<review>I've done somewhere between 15-20 escape rooms around the West Coast, and this is one of the top 2 for "best aesthetic." All the puzzles tie into the theme, even some of the introduction stuff is tied in, which really adds to the fun of the event. There were some REALLY cool surprises I didn't see coming.

And to the puzzles. I believe this is the first escape room these 2 gentlemen have created, and it's really very good for a 1st room. They've done their research, created good puzzles, and are continually tweaking to make the experience flow.  There were some super satisfying puzzles in there, including some puzzles of which I'd never seen the like. The puzzles were varied enough that everybody got a crack at a different type of puzzle.

My main critique, they've already fixed and disclaimed to us when we arrived: We booked our room when the website said 4-6 people, and 6 is far too many for experienced players. We should have come with 4 people. But I believe they've capped it now. So if you've done escape rooms before and have been successful, go with the min number of players.<//review><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOwW4W_yog7LZIZcW0tW6vurybkY7X0Iqs-6Z4O=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMArVR1AVhK-k6shC0zmn6C4GaLbjOVemlsrUDG=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures><response>None</response><gmap_id>0x808431c7cea84dc3:0x5e3b6e14d6815555< /gmap_id></record>

< review>
I took my car here twice, first time to repair brakes there were rusted up from the decade of winters and seasons in Chicago. Job well done. This last time was another thing entirely, since it was a story of revival, or more aptly in October, resurrection.

Basically, some components of the engine assembly were rusted and worn out and failing. Car was dead. Won't start. It happens. Some of them were overdue for inspection and replacement, my bad. It required only a few parts to replace and tune up for the fix.

I took it another place I shall not name down the street where I was told the engine is "dead, it won't turn. It is an older engine and not a very common car thus is $3k plus labor it would be $4k total. or. we can buy it for $200." Dead. Silence. I knew something was up, had it towed here to get it checked out, professionally, and so glad I did.

The engine does turn now. Turns out is was mainly the A/C compressor being frozen, not allowing the engine to turn over. Also, the acc belt tensioner assy. Either way, whatever it was, they did it, worked fast, and accommodated the tow truck, ordering parts to ship is to the shop and constant communication throughout the entire experience.

Highly recommend Oceanworks for any auto, mechanical, electrical, tuning up, whatever your needs are, this is the auto shop!<//review>

We had two jags chain smoking cigars with no regard for anyone else. I guess that's what makes cigar smokers so special. Anyway, if you can't find any other food, this will pass. Cheese and crackers from Safeway will save you a bunch of money and be about as palatable.<//Review>

<time>1588529671183</time><Pictures>None</Pictures><GmapID>0x8083e84859f93f01:0x240c8f59b149de94</GmapID><user>110086006161580002252< /user>< Name>
Selecter jd< /Name>
<Review>It seems the restaurant is under new management as of Feb. 2020 (just in time for the Shelter in Place) and my experiences there all occurred previously to the change.  I'll have to drag myself in there when the Corona thing has passed (if they are still open) and write an updated review.  So take this for what it's worth.

The boathouse is a great place if you like to drink at the bar or come up from the water in a boat to drink on the deck.  They certainly seem to try hard at making a nice restaurant looking at the menu items and selection but when the place is absolutely empty except for your party and it takes over an hour to serve three main dishes and they are cold and stale you have to wonder what the problem is.  At least this has been my experience about a dozen times over the last 4-5 years.

Sure the dining room is quite dated and could use a deep cleaning, I don't mind that.  Also, the staff seem like well meaning people who are trying their best but if you're gonna run a restaurant the guests need hot fresh food in a timely manner.  Now if you're a drinker perhaps you can knock back a couple of high balls and by the time the food comes you're too buzzed to care that it's not hot or it has been an hour and a half after you received your salad/soup/app or isn't fresh and flavorful even if there are only the three or four of your group in the entire restaurant.  In fact reading through some of the 5 star reviews you might notice how many times the 'great bartender' is mentioned or the pool table or that many of the food items mentioned are basically deep fried bar food..

Now the place does have a pretty regular and busy section but that is in the bar/deck.  Since I haven't been a drinker in a long time I couldn't comment on that part but they do seem to be having a pretty good time by the sound.  The Boat House to me is like an old school Bar and Grill where the grill is there when the bar crowd need something to eat long after the Happy Hour has past.    My best experiences have been ordering take out and would suggest this to anyone focused on the food.  Sure it's usually cold by the time you get it home but you expect that.  They also generally have it ready to go when you show up.

I'm not trying to be negative this is just my honest in my assessment.  I've worked in nearly a dozen restaurants over the years and eaten at a few too.  I also live about three blocks from the place.  The only reason I've frequented the place regularly is that my parents always want to go there when visiting because it's on the lake, despite my protestations.< /Review><rate>2</rate>< response>

<userid>114713462113277205212< /userid>< username>
Featherbed Railroad Bed & Breakfast< /username>
< date>
1385652739709< /date>
< Rate>
5</Rate>
< text>
The Boathouse has been a staple for guests for some time now but recently new management took over the kitchen and really stepped up the menu and service. The food can best be described as comfort food with barbecue as well and a number of intriguing daily specials. There's a full bar as well with a view of Clear Lake plus outdoor seating in the summer with bands featured  on Sunday afternoons.

Recently we had some sandwiches delivered which is usually unremarkable but I happened to get the tri tip sandwich. Bottom line, the tri tip had a wonderful smoky flavor and was as tender as can be. I avoid tri tip sandwiches because you usually end up with gristle surprise which ruins the experience - not in this case. It was tender and meaty from bite one to the end. The only disappointment was having finished the sandwich, darnit. But they'll make more!

We have sent many guests down the street to the Boathouse and have heard plenty of very positive reviews of the food and service. Being regulars ourselves we can attest to the warm atmosphere of this local hangout. The food is consistent and good, prices are very fair and service is generally quite good as well. We're pretty fortunate to have such a cool local hangout just a few steps down the street from us.</text>
